---
title: "Sound and video issues + freezes after software update"
date: 2016-01-25
forum: General Help
---

### Post by KIAaze on 2016-01-25
I'm using Kubuntu 15.10 with the kubuntu backports repository.
Two days ago, I used the KDE software updater instead of using apt-get update/upgrade as I usualy do (in case that matters).
The biggest change seems to have been an upgrade to Plasma 5.5.3.

Since I rebooted after those upgrades, I had several issues:

1) No sound. KDE does not seem to detect any sound cards or devices and just lists a "dummy output". However, the sound still works when booting into an older Ubuntu install (I have multiple distros installed), so it does not seem to be a hardware issue.
I managed to get audi working again once, by re-enabling the kmix system tray icon, making it run on startup and rebooting.
However today, after a new boot, the sound is gone again, despite the kmix icon being there.

2) VLC does not fit played videos to the window size anymore and only shows a small image. Same when trying to run it fullscreen. Other players like dragon player appear to work.

3) I had at least 2-3 complete freezes, which forced me to use alt+printscreen+REISUB to reboot. Nothing else seemed to work, including switching to other ttys.
The freezes seem to happen when running anything apt-get related, although not always.

Has anybody else recently had similar issues?
For VLC, I'm suspecting some ffmpeg or wayland stuff, but I don't even know if I'm already using wayland or not. O.o

Here is my dpkg.log:
Problems started appearing after the updates on 2016-01-23.
I just started an apt-get install cinnamon-desktop-environment, hoping that it won't freeze and that my problems only come from KDE/Plasma. (although I already tested with OpenBox, which had the same problems, so unlikely, but before doing an OS re-install, I though I might as well try out a few more things).

### Post by KIAaze on 2016-01-30
To add to the list of issues:
4) Kubuntu asks for password when plugging in USB
5) Shutdown via KDE menu (application launcher) not working anymore. It only logs me out and I have to shutdown from the SDDM login screen
6) Switching to virtual terminals via ctrl+alt+Fn keys does not work anymore.

So maybe it's a policykit issue, I don't know.

### Post by cathect2 on 2016-01-30
I'm having a similar issue, I think. Started just a few days ago after an update.

 I'm using Ubuntu 15.10. My problem seems related to USB. Like you, my usb-connected external audio card is not recognized. When I boot, there is clearly a moment when USB is being accessed (my usb mic starts blinking) and this seems to paralyze the computer for several minutes and will not allow me to log in until it moves past this usb issue (light stops blinking on my mic). Once logged in, I have an invisible mouse, no sound. When rebooting, I get "usb_set_interface_failed" messages.

I think this is definitely software-related. I have a brand new, right out of the box, System76 machine that this happened to right after its first update. Because of this issue, I went back to my old machine. After performing an update, the problem appeared there too.

---

### Post by KIAaze on 2016-02-01
Well, I finally gave up and just re-installed Ubuntu 15.10, this time with Gnome 3/shell...

Sound works, USB mounting without password works and no freezes so far.
I even quite like the Activities dashboard. :)

I guess KDE5 is not mature enough yet, just as KDE4 and Gnome 3 were a few years ago.
Although my desktop PC with Kubuntu 15.10 seems to have survived the updates, so either it's hardware related or some custom config on my laptop messed everything up.

For what it's worth, while trying to debug my Kubuntu laptop in recovery mode, I got loads of these error messages:
```
Error getting authority: Error initializing authority: Could not connect: No such file or directory (g-io-error-quark, 1)
```
